SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[Brand], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[Description], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[StockQuantity], [c].[Id], [p0].[Id], [p0].[Image], [p0].[MainImage], [p0].[ProductId], [p1].[Id], [p1].[Name], [p1].[ProductId], [p1].[Value], [c].[ImageUrl], [c].[Name], [t].[Id], [t].[DiscountId], [t].[ProductId], [t].[Id0], [t].[DiscountPercentage], [t].[EndDate], [t].[Name], [t].[StartDate]
FROM [Products] AS [p]
INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [p].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [ProductImages] AS [p0] ON [p].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN [ProductFeatures] AS [p1] ON [p].[Id] = [p1].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d].[Id], [d].[DiscountId], [d].[ProductId], [d0].[Id] AS [Id0], [d0].[DiscountPercentage], [d0].[EndDate], [d0].[Name], [d0].[StartDate]
    FROM [DiscountProducts] AS [d]
    INNER JOIN [Discounts] AS [d0] ON [d].[DiscountId] = [d0].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [p].[Id] = [t].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [p].[Id], [c].[Id], [p0].[Id], [p1].[Id], [t].[Id]

SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[Brand], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[Description], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[StockQuantity], [c].[Id], [p0].[Id], [p0].[Image], [p0].[MainImage], [p0].[ProductId], [p1].[Id], [p1].[Name], [p1].[ProductId], [p1].[Value], [c].[ImageUrl], [c].[Name], [t].[Id], [t].[DiscountId], [t].[ProductId], [t].[Id0], [t].[DiscountPercentage], [t].[EndDate], [t].[Name], [t].[StartDate]
FROM [Products] AS [p]
INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [p].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [ProductImages] AS [p0] ON [p].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN [ProductFeatures] AS [p1] ON [p].[Id] = [p1].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d].[Id], [d].[DiscountId], [d].[ProductId], [d0].[Id] AS [Id0], [d0].[DiscountPercentage], [d0].[EndDate], [d0].[Name], [d0].[StartDate]
    FROM [DiscountProducts] AS [d]
    INNER JOIN [Discounts] AS [d0] ON [d].[DiscountId] = [d0].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [p].[Id] = [t].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [p].[Id], [c].[Id], [p0].[Id], [p1].[Id], [t].[Id]

FROM [Products] AS [p]

) AS [t] ON [p].[Id] = [t].[ProductId]

INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [p].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [ProductImages] AS [p0] ON [p].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN [ProductFeatures] AS [p1] ON [p].[Id] = [p1].[ProductId]

    SELECT [d].[Id], [d].[DiscountId], [d].[ProductId], [d0].[Id] AS [Id0], [d0].[DiscountPercentage], [d0].[EndDate], [d0].[Name], [d0].[StartDate]
